Disadvantages: The facilities are old, the bathtub in the room I live in can't hold water, and the master has repaired it three times but still can't fix it; there is a seam on the edge of the balcony door, which can't be closed tightly; there is a gap on the edge of the anti-mosquito curtain; the cold water is relatively small; The young man who cleaned the house was very serious, but the aunt who cleaned the house in the next few days was perfunctory. But these problems are nothing compared to the price and advantages, and the flaws are not concealed. I stayed with my child for a week and was quite satisfied.
